     water supply system. Will they be replaced in   risk to public health, the use of asbestos-containing materials is minimized by excluding
     the upcoming project? Why asbestos-             such materials from new construction/rehabilitation. All safety precautions for handling
     containing materials are prohibited?            such materials will be applied during the rehabilitation of water supply systems:
                                                     immediate removal of the material for burial, application of safety measures by workers.
                                                     Since the risk to health from asbestos is now widely recognized, global health
                                                     organizations and workers' associations, research institutes and some governments have
                                                     banned its commercial use. The World Bank expects Borrowers and other clients in all

13   How were the villages selected? What criteria   The list was provided by the Cabinet of Ministers of the Kyrgyz Republic represented by
     were used to select villages?                   the State Institution for the Development of Drinking Water Supply and Wastewater
                                                     Disposal of the Water Resources Service under the Ministry of Water Resources,
                                                     Agriculture and Processing Industry of the Kyrgyz Republic according to the following
                                                     criteria:
                                                     •     lack of reliable water supply systems (in some areas) where people rely on unsafe
                                                           sources\systems;
                                                     •     outdated and poor infrastructure (built more than 40 years ago, no overhaul and
                                                           upgrading of infrastructure);
                                                     •     low quality of service (water supply less than 3 hours, poor water quality, low/high
                                                           pressure);
                                                     •     limited management and operational capacity of organizations and enterprises
                                                           operating water supply and wastewater disposal systems.
14   Will the ecology in our neighborhood be         The risks of pollution, contamination and depletion of natural resources are unlikely. Risk
     seriously affected by the upcoming project?     management will be implemented through preventive environmental measures and
                                                     regular environmental monitoring. For each subproject, an “Environmental Protection”
                                                     section will be prepared, which will have to undergo state environmental assessment, and
                                                     an Environmental and Social Management Plan will also be prepared. The project will
                                                     provide for mitigation activities, and will also provide a budget for these activities.

19   If irreversible private land acquisition is     Land acquisition and resettlement of any kind needs to be avoided, or if they cannot be
     required during construction, what              avoided, they need to be minimized by considering all possible options. In the event of
     compensation will the landowner receive?        land acquisition, a replacement plot of land of equivalent market value, acceptable to the
                                                     Affected Person, shall be provided as a priority option and shall be appropriate in area and
                                                     fertility to the land withdrawn. In the absence of available land, cash compensation at
                                                     replacement cost will be paid, and the costs of fees for registration and re-registration of
                                                     rights and costs to prepare the land to a condition similar to that of the land affected by
                                                     the project. If the remainder of the land plot is no longer usable, the entire land plot must
                                                     be purchased.
